Cν_def : Gamma_nu_nabla_mu M r θ μ ν a b = Cνa + Cνb

          dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ e μ b) r θ * g M a e r θ) +

  fun ρ =>
    -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν a) r θ * g M ρ b r θ +

Cν_def : Gamma_nu_nabla_mu M r θ μ ν a b = Cνa + Cνb

  sumIdx B_b - Cμa + Cνa =

    0
